# OpenCursor 3,000 Feature Masterlist

Total features: **3000**

## Domain Distribution
- AI Features: 900
- Agent Workflow and Automation: 650
- Editor UX and Productivity: 500
- Collaboration and Team Workflows: 250
- Integrations and Extensibility: 220
- Performance and Reliability: 180
- Security, Privacy, and Governance: 150
- Enterprise/Admin Controls: 100
- Onboarding, Learning, and Discoverability: 50

## AI Features

1. `AI-0001` | **Enable Model Orchestration capability 1 for ai features**
   - Description: Deliver model orchestration improvements in ai features with configurable thresholds, optimized for offline-first setups.
   - Priority: `P1`
   - Complexity: `M`
2. `AI-0002` | **Implement Prompt Engineering capability 2 for ai features**
   - Description: Deliver prompt engineering improvements in ai features with team-level controls, optimized for legacy modernization programs.
